caAERS CAAERS-3133 Rules returning reports affiliated with other study sites Bug Closed Critical Fixed Ramachandra Rao Seethiraju paul.baumgartner 10/15/2009 16:47 11/11/2009 14:03 Version 1.9.6 Version 2.0 Module 12: Rules / Automated Decision Support
Module 4: Adverse Event Reporting		 30-Oct-09 0                 This is required to support hosted mode effectively.

Currently, the rules are returning any reports that are affiliated with any organization associated with the study. The rules should ONLY return reports associated with the Sponsor organization, Coordinating Center, and the Site organization that the subject is associated with.

This is required to ensure that the rules does not return a recommendation for completing a WFU IRB report on a subject from Mayo. Currently, this scenario can occur.

caAERS CAAERS-3109 CAAERS-3105
Rename and add functionality to List Report Definitions section		 Sub-task Resolved Major Fixed David Coffey Sameer Sawant 10/7/2009 14:12 11/5/2009 14:19   Version 2.0     0                 To be consistent with the rules, "List Report Definitions" should be renamed to "Manage Report Definitions".

Also the section "Import Report Definition" will be removed and it will be moved to "Manage Report Definitions" page as a collapsable section under the list of report definitions.
Also there should be a link saying "Create" that takes the user to "Create Report Definition" flow.		            
caAERS CAAERS-3108 CAAERS-3105
Updates to the "Create Rule flow"		 Sub-task Closed Major Fixed karthik.iyer@semanticbits.com Sameer Sawant 10/7/2009 14:04 11/2/2009 16:11   Version 2.0     0                 As mentioned in Issue CAAERS-3106, Manage Rules will be modified to be "Create Rules".
Currently this flow comprises of four steps, namely,
1. Rule Level
2. Rule Set
3. Rules
4. Review

This will now be modified. The first 2 steps will be merged as there is not much information being gathered under step 2. The new steps will be -
1. Select type
2. Define rule
3. Review

Also "Define Rule" will have a "Save and Continue". This is needed as initially there was a "Save" button at the end of the flow under the Review page. This page used to be very long and it was easy for the user to miss the Save button and exit the flow without actually saving the rule. This was annoying.		            
caAERS CAAERS-3107 CAAERS-3105

Sub-task Closed Major Fixed karthik.iyer@semanticbits.com Sameer Sawant 10/7/2009 13:58 11/10/2009 17:30   Version 2.0     0                 The user should be able to "Import rules" in Manage Rules page. Thus we get rid of the section "Import Rules". This will now be a minimizable section below the list of rules in the Manage Rules page.
Also there should be a "Create" button for creating new rules. Clicking this button will take the user to the "Create Rules" flow.

caAERS CAAERS-3016 Mismatch of Amendment # between caAERS and AdEERS Bug Closed Blocker Fixed karthik.iyer@semanticbits.com paul.baumgartner 9/29/2009 13:40 11/5/2009 11:06 Version 1.9.6 Version 1.9.6 Module 4: Adverse Event Reporting 30-Sep-09 0                 Summary of Issue:
There is a mismatch in how caAERS and AdEERS handle amendments that are withdrawn. caAERS rolls back the amendment number if a report is withdrawn, whereas AdEERS does not. This will result in a rejection of report submission from caAERS to AdEERS if there was a previously withdrawn 24hr amendment.

Proposed Fix:
The proposed fix is that caAERS would be changed to handle withdrawn amendments the same as AdEERS, meaning that withdrawn amendments would not rollback the amendment number. This would also require a change to the business rule enforced by AdEERS to allow submissions from caAERS to have an amendment number that is greater than a previous amendment number, but not necessarily sequential to the previous amendment number. Allowing non-sequential amendment numbers would be required since AdEERS will not know about amendments started in caAERS but withdrawn prior to submission.

Module 4: Adverse Event Reporting		 21-Oct-09 0                 caAERS needs to support a new AE coding terminology, the CTCAE v4.0. Multiple file formats of the current version are available at the following URL: http://evs.nci.nih.gov/ftp1/CTCAE

CTCAE v4.0
Category is MedDRA SystemOrganClass (SOC) (can map to CtcCategory.name)
No Short Names
No Supra-ordinate terms or Select terms
Terms are coded to MedDRA Lower Level Term (LLT) codes (can map to CtcTerm.ctepCode)
Terms have definitions (new field)
